<p>Additionally, the <span class="katex--inline">KaTeX parse error: Undefined control sequence: \appox at position 1: \Ã≤aÃ≤pÃ≤pÃ≤oÃ≤xÃ≤</span> symbol is <em>transitive:</em><sup class="footnote-ref"><a href="#fn7" id="fnref7">7</a></sup> if <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>P</mi><mi>r</mi><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo>‚âà</mo><mi>P</mi><mi>r</mi><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Pr[X]\approx Pr[Y]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚âà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>P</mi><mi>r</mi><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo>‚âà</mo><mi>P</mi><mi>r</mi><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>Z</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Pr[Y]\approx Pr[Z]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚âà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">Z</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>, then <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>P</mi><mi>r</mi><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo>‚âà</mo><mi>P</mi><mi>r</mi><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>Z</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Pr[X]\approx Pr[Z]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚âà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">Z</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> (perhaps with a lightly larger, but still negligible, difference).</p>
<h2 id="indistinguishability">4.3 Indistinguishability</h2>
<p>So far we have been writing formal security definitions in terms of interchangeable libraries, which requires that two libraries have <em>exactly</em> the <em>same</em> effect on <em>every</em> calling program. Going forward, our security definitions will not be quite as demanding. First, we only consider polynomial-time calling programs; second, we don‚Äôt require the libraries to have exactly the same effect on the calling program, only that the difference in effects is negligible.</p>
<p><strong>Definition 4.5 (Indistinguishable)</strong><br>
Let <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> be two libraries with a common interface. We say that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> are indistinguishable, and write   <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo>‚âà</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\approx\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚âà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> , if for all polynomial-time programs <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span></span></span></span></span> that output a single bit, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mo>‚âà</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 1\right] \approx \operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {right }} \Rightarrow 1\right]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚âà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p>We call the quantity <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mo>‚àí</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 1\right] -\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {right }} \Rightarrow 1\right]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚àí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span></span></span></span></span> he advantage or bias of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span></span></span></span></span> in distinguishing <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> from <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. Two libraries are therefore indistinguishable if all polynomial-time calling programs have negligible advantage in distinguishing them.</p>
<p>From the properties of the ‚Äú<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>‚âà</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\approx</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.48312em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚âà</span></span></span></span></span>‚Äù symbol, we can see that indistinguishability of libraries is also transitive, which allows us to carry out hybrid proofs of security in the same way as before.</p>
<p><strong>Example</strong><br>
Here is a very simple example of two indistinguishable libraries:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable accentunder="true"><mrow><mtext>PREDICT</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‚Äæ</mo></munder></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>s</mi><mo>‚Üê</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0</mn></mstyle><mo separator="true">,</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>1</mn></mstyle><msup><mo stretchy="false">}</mo><mi>Œª</mi></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable rowspacing="0.6599999999999999em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em" rowlines="solid none"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mspace width="1em"></mspace><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><munder accentunder="true"><mrow><mtext>PREDICT</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‚Äæ</mo></munder></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace \def\arraystretch{1.5}
\begin{array}{|l|}\hline
\quad \quad\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\\\hline
\underline{\text{PREDICT}(x):}\\
\quad s\leftarrow\{\textcolor{brown}{0},\textcolor{brown}{1}\}^\lambda\\
\quad \text{return}\ x\stackrel{?}{=} s\\\hline
\end{array}\quad \begin{array}{|l|}\hline
\quad \quad \mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}\\\hline
\underline{\text{PREDICT}(x):}\\
\quad \text{return false}\\\hline
\end{array}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 7.25em; vertical-align: -3.35em;"></span><span class="underline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.35em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.26em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">return&nbsp;false</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.45em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="vertical-separator" style="height: 5.4em; 0.05em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -6.1em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 4.95em;"></span><span class="hline" style="border-bottom-width: 0.05em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -7.9em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 4.95em;"></span><span class="hline" style="border-bottom-width: 0.05em;"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.45em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
Imagine the calling program trying to predict which string will be chosen when uniformly sampling from <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0</mn></mstyle><mo separator="true">,</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>1</mn></mstyle><msup><mo stretchy="false">}</mo><mi>Œª</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{\textcolor{brown}{0},\textcolor{brown}{1}\}^\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">Œª</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. The left library tells the calling program whether its prediction was correct. The right library doesn‚Äôt even bother sampling a string, it just always says ‚Äúsorry, your prediction was wrong.‚Äù</p>
<p>Here is one obvious strategy (maybe not the best one, we will see) to distinguish these libraries. The calling program <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}_{\text{obvious}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> calls predict many times and outputs 1 if it ever received true as a response. Since it seems like the argument to predict might not have any effect, let‚Äôs just use the string of all-<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0</mn></mstyle></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\textcolor{brown}{0}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span></span></span></span></span> as argument every time.</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable rowspacing="0.6599999999999999em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em" rowlines="solid none none none"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mspace width="2em"></mspace><mspace width="1em"></mspace><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious</mtext></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mtext>do&nbsp;</mtext><mi>q</mi><mtext>&nbsp;times:</mtext></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mtext>if&nbsp;PREDICT</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0</mn></mstyle><mi>Œª</mi></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mtext>true</mtext></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mtext>return&nbsp;</mtext><mn>1</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mtext>return&nbsp;</mtext><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></menclose></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\def\arraystretch{1.5}
\begin{array}{|l|}\hline
\quad \qquad \quad\mathcal{A}_{\text{obvious}}\\\hline
\text{do}\ q\ \text{times:}\\
\quad\text{if PREDICT}(\textcolor{brown}{0}^\lambda)=\text{true} \\
\quad \quad\text{return}\ 1\\
\text{return}\ 0\\\hline
\end{array}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 9.05em; vertical-align: -4.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 4.8em;"><span class="" style="top: -6.75em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 6.75em;"></span><span class="mtable"><span class="vertical-separator" style="height: 9em; vertical-align: -4.25em;"></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 4.75em;"><span class="" style="top: -6.75em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.26em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 2em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -4.95em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.26em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">do</span></span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">times:</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.15em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.26em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">if&nbsp;PREDICT</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">Œª</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">true</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.35em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.26em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">return</span></span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: 0.45em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.26em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">return</span></span><span class="mspace">&nbsp;</span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 4.25em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="vertical-separator" style="height: 9em; vertical-align: -4.25em;"></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.5em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 6.75em;"></span><span class="hline" style="border-bottom-width: 0.05em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -9.7em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 6.75em;"></span><span class="hline" style="border-bottom-width: 0.05em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -11.5em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 6.75em;"></span><span class="hline" style="border-bottom-width: 0.05em;"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 4.25em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul>
<li><em><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> can never return true, so <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mtext>Pr</mtext><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious</mtext></msub><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Pr}[\mathcal{A}_{\text{obvious}}\diamond\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}\Rightarrow 1]=0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Pr</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span></em></li>
<li><em>In <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> each call to PREDICT has an independent probability <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>Œª</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1/2^\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">Œª</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> of returning true. So <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mtext>Pr</mtext><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious</mtext></msub><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Pr}[\mathcal{A}_{\text{obvious}}\diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\Rightarrow 1]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Pr</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> is surely non-zero. Actually, the exact probability is a bit cumbersome to write:</em><br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.24999999999999992em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>‚àí</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>0</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>‚àí</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mtext>&nbsp;all&nbsp;</mtext><mi>q</mi><mtext>&nbsp;independent&nbsp;calls&nbsp;to&nbsp;PREDICT&nbsp;return&nbsp;</mtext><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">l</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">s</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">e</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>‚àí</mo><msup><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>‚àí</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>Œª</mi></msup></mfrac><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mi>q</mi></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A}_{\text {obvious }} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 1\right]&amp;=1-\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A}_{\text {obvious }} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 0\right]\\
&amp;=1-\operatorname{Pr}[\text { all } q \text { independent calls to PREDICT return } \mathrm{false}]\\
&amp;=1-\left(1-\frac{1}{2^{\lambda}}\right)^{q}
\end{aligned}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 5.75432em; vertical-align: -2.62716em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 3.12716em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.79145em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.50429em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -4.29145em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.50429em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.12716em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.62716em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
Rather than understand this probability, we can just compute an upper bound for it. Using the union bound, we get:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.24999999999999992em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>‚©Ω</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mtext>&nbsp;first&nbsp;call&nbsp;to&nbsp;PREDICT&nbsp;returns&nbsp;true&nbsp;</mtext><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mtext>&nbsp;second&nbsp;call&nbsp;to&nbsp;PREDICT&nbsp;returns&nbsp;true&nbsp;</mtext><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo>+</mo><mo>‚ãØ</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>q</mi><mfrac><mn>1</mn><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>Œª</mi></msup></mfrac></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A}_{\text {obvious }} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 1\right]&amp; \leqslant \operatorname{Pr}[\text { first call to PREDICT returns true }] \\
&amp;+\operatorname{Pr}[\text { second call to PREDICT returns true }]+\cdots \\
&amp;=q \frac{1}{2^{\lambda}}
\end{aligned}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 5.30744em; vertical-align: -2.40372em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.90372em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.38516em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.32144em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" amsrm">‚©Ω</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span
