mtight">Œª</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.686em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.40372em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
This is an overestimate of some probabilities (e.g., if the rst call to predict returns true, then the second call isn‚Äôt made). More fundamentally, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>Œª</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q/2^\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">Œª</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>  exceeds 1 when <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span></span> is large. But nevertheless, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mtext>Pr</mtext><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious</mtext></msub><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo>‚©Ω</mo><mi>q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>Œª</mi></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Pr}[\mathcal{A}_{\text{obvious}}\diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\Rightarrow 1]\leqslant q/2^\lambda.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Pr</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel amsrm">‚©Ω</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">Œª</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p><em>We showed that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}_{\text{obvious}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> has non-zero advantage. This is enough to show that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">‚â†</mi><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\neq\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel"><span class="mord"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.69444em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mrel">ÓÄ†</span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.19444em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>.<br>
We also showed that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}_{\text{obvious}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> has advantage at most <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>Œª</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q/2^\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">Œª</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. Since <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}_{\text{obvious}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> runs in polynomial<br>
time, it can only make a polynomial number q of queries to the library, so <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>Œª</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q/2^\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">Œª</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is negligible. However, this is not enough to show that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo>‚âà</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\approx\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚âà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> since it considers only <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> single calling program. To show that the libraries are indistinguishable, we must show that <strong>every</strong> calling program‚Äôs advantage is negligible.</em></p>
<p>In a few pages, we will prove that for any <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span></span></span></span></span> that makes <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span></span> calls to PREDICT,<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo fence="true">‚à£</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mo>‚àí</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mo fence="true">‚à£</mo></mrow><mo>‚©Ω</mo><mfrac><mi>q</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>Œª</mi></msup></mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\left|\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{F} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 1\right]-\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {right }} \Rightarrow 1\right]\right| \leqslant \frac{q}{2^{\lambda}}.
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">‚à£</span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.09931em;">F</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚àí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">‚à£</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel amsrm">‚©Ω</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.79356em; vertical-align: -0.686em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.10756em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.775108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.989em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">Œª</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.686em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
For any polynomial-time <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span></span></span></span></span>, the number <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span></span> of calls to PREDICT will be a polynomial in <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>Œª</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">Œª</span></span></span></span></span>, making <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>Œª</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q/2^\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">Œª</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> a negligible function. Hence, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo>‚âà</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\approx\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚âà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<h3 id="other-properties">Other Properties</h3>
<p><strong>Lemma 4.6(<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>‚âà</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\bf{\approx}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.48312em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mrel">‚âà</span></span></span></span></span></span></span> facts)</strong><br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mtext>&nbsp;If&nbsp;</mtext><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>‚â°</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mtext>&nbsp;then&nbsp;</mtext><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>‚âà</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mtext>&nbsp;Also,&nbsp;if&nbsp;</mtext><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>‚âà</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>‚âà</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mtext>&nbsp;then&nbsp;</mtext><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>‚âà</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\text { If } \mathcal{L}_{1} \equiv \mathcal{L}_{2} \text { then } \mathcal{L}_{1} \approx \mathcal{L}_{2} . \text { Also, if } \mathcal{L}_{1} \approx \mathcal{L}_{2} \approx \mathcal{L}_{3} \text { then } \mathcal{L}_{1} \approx \mathcal{L}_{3}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;If&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚â°</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
Analogous to Lemma 2.11, we also have the following library chaining lemma, which you are asked to prove as an exercise:</p>
<p><strong>Lemma 4.7 (Chaining)</strong><br>
If <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo>‚âà</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\approx\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚âà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> then <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mo>‚àó</mo></msup><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo>‚âà</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mo>‚àó</mo></msup><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}^*\diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\approx\mathcal{L}^*\diamond\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.688696em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">‚àó</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> for any polynomial-time library <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mo>‚àó</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}^*</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.688696em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">‚àó</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<h3 id="bad-event-lemma">Bad-Event Lemma</h3>
<p>A common situation is when two libraries are expected to execute exactly the same statements, until some rare &amp; exceptional condition happens. In that case, we can bound an attacker‚Äôs distinguishing advantage by the probability of the exceptional condition.</p>
<p>More formally,</p>
<p><strong>Lemma 4.8 (Bad events)</strong><br>
<em>Let <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> be libraries that each dene a variable named ‚Äòbad‚Äô that is initialized to 0. If <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>  have identical code, except for code blocks reachable only when bad = 1 (e.g., guarded by an ‚Äúif bad = 1‚Äù statement), then</em></p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo fence="true">‚à£</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mo>‚àí</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>‚áí</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mo fence="true">‚à£</mo></mrow><mo>‚©Ω</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>‚Å°</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mo>‚ãÑ</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mtext>&nbsp;sets&nbsp;bad&nbsp;</mtext><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\left|\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 1\right]-\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {right }} \Rightarrow 1\right]\right| \leqslant \operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \text { sets bad }=1\right]
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">‚à£</span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚àí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">‚à£</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel amsrm">‚©Ω</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚ãÑ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;sets&nbsp;bad&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><strong><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>‚ãÜ</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\bf{\star}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.46528em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord">‚ãÜ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span>Proof</strong><br>
Fix an arbitrary calling program <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span></span></span></span></span>. In this proof, we use conditional probabilites<sup class="footnote-ref"><a href="#fn7" id="fnref7:1">7</a></sup> to isolate the cases where bad is changed to 1. We define the following events:</p>
<hr class="footnotes-sep">
<section class="footnotes">
<ol class="footnotes-list">
<li id="fn1" class="footnote-item"><p>The original letters, handwritten by Nash, are available at: <a href="https://www.nsa.gov/Portals/70/documents/news-features/declassified-documents/nash-letters/nash_letters1.pdf.">https://www.nsa.gov/Portals/70/documents/news-features/declassified-documents/nash-letters/nash_letters1.pdf.</a> <a href="#fnref1" class="footnote-backref">‚Ü©Ô∏é</a></p>
</li>
<li id="fn2" class="footnote-item"><p>Nash originally used r to denote the length of the key, in bits. In all of the excerpts quoted in this chapter, I have translated his mathematical expressions into our notation (<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>Œª</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">Œª</span></span></span></span></span>). <a href="#fnref2" class="footnote-backref">‚Ü©Ô∏é</a></p>
</li>
<li id="fn3" class="footnote-item"><p>As of October 2018, the cheapest class of CPU that is suitable for an intensive computation is the m5.large, which is a 2.5 GHz CPU. Such a CPU performs <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mn>2</mn><mn>43</mn></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2^{43}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.814108em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">4</span><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> clock cycles per hour. The cheapest rate on<br>
EC2 for this CPU is 0.044 USD per hour (3-year reserved instances, all costs paid upfront). All in all, the cost for a single clock cycle (rounding down) is <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mn>2</mn><mrow><mo>‚àí</mo><mn>48</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2^{-48}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.814108em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">‚àí</span><span class="mord mtight">4</span><span class="mord mtight">8</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> USD. <a href="#fnref3" class="footnote-backref">‚Ü©Ô∏é</a></p>
</li>
<li id="fn4" class="footnote-item"><p>I found some estimates (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gross_world_product">https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gross_world_product</a>) of the gross world product (like the GDP but for the entire world) throughout human history, and summed them up for every year. <a href="#fnref4" class="footnote-backref">‚Ü©Ô∏é</a></p>
</li>
<li id="fn5" class="footnote-item"><p><a href="https://arstechnica.com/information-technology/2017/02/at-deaths-door-for-years-widely-used-sha1-function-is-now-dead/">https://arstechnica.com/information-technology/2017/02/at-deaths-door-for-years-widely-used-sha1-function-is-now-dead/</a> <a href="#fnref5" class="footnote-backref">‚Ü©Ô∏é</a></p>
</li>
<li id="fn6" class="footnote-item"><p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>P</mi><mi>r</mi><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo>‚âà</mo><mi>P</mi><mi>r</mi><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Pr[A] \approx Pr[B]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathdefault">A</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚âà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> doesn‚Äôt mean that events <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">A</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span> almost always happen together (when <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">A</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span> are defined over a common probability space) ‚Äî imagine <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">A</span></span></span></span></span> being the event ‚Äúthe coin came up heads‚Äù and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span> being the event ‚Äúthe coin came up tails.‚Äù These events have the same probability but never happen together. To say that ‚Äú<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">A</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span> almost always happen together,‚Äù you‚Äôd have to say something like <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>P</mi><mi>r</mi><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo>‚âà</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Pr[A\oplus B]\approx 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathdefault">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚âà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>, where <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A \oplus B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.76666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span> denotes the event that exactly one of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">A</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span> happens. <a href="#fnref6" class="footnote-backref">‚Ü©Ô∏é</a></p>
</li>
<li id="fn7" class="footnote-item"><p>The use of c <a href="#fnref7" class="footnote-backref">‚Ü©Ô∏é</a> <a href="#fnref7:1" class="footnote-backref">‚Ü©Ô∏é</a></p>
